269→func handleRootHealth(name string, firstTimeHealthy func(), checks ...HealthChecker) http.HandlerFunc {\n   270→\tvar notifyOnce sync.Once\n   271→\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   272→\t\texcluded := getExcludedChecks(r)\n   273→\t\tunknownExcluded := excluded.Clone()\n   274→\t\t// failedVerboseLogOutput is for output to the log. charset=utf-8\")\n   323→\t\tw.Header().Set(\"X-Content-Type-Options\", \"nosniff\")\n   324→\t\tif _, found := r.URL.Query()[\"verbose\"]; !found {\n   325→\t\t\tfmt.Fprint(w, \"ok\")\n   326→\t\t\treturn\n   327→\t\t}\n   328→\n   329→\t\tindividualCheckOutput.WriteTo(w)\n   330→\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"%s check passed\\n\", name)\n   331→\t}\n   332→}\n   333→\n   334→// adaptCheckToHandler returns an http.HandlerFunc that serves the provided checks.\n   335→func adaptCheckToHandler(c func(r *http.Request) error) http.HandlerFunc {\n   336→\treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   337→\t\terr := c(r)\n   338→\t\tif err != nil {\n   339→\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"internal server error: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n   340→\t\t} else {\n   341→\t\t\tfmt.Fprint(w, \"ok\")\n   342→\t\t}\n   343→\t})\n   344→}\n   345→\n   346→// checkerNames returns the names of the checks in the same order as passed in.\n   347→func checkerNames(checks ...HealthChecker) []string {\n   348→\t// accumulate the names of checks for printing them out.\n   349→\tcheckerNames := make([]string, 0, len(checks))\n   350→\tfor _, check := range checks {\n   351→\t\tcheckerNames = append(checkerNames, check.Name())\n   352→\t}\n   353→\treturn checkerNames\n   354→}\n   355→\n   356→// formatQuoted returns a formatted string of the health check names,\n   357→// preserving the order passed in.\n   358→func formatQuoted(names ...string) string {\n   359→\tquoted := make([]string, 0, len(names))\n   360→\tfor _, name := range names {\n   361→\t\tquoted = append(quoted, fmt.Sprintf(\"%q\", name))\n   362→\t}\n   363→\treturn strings.Join(quoted, \",\")\n   364→}\n   365→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. semantics:\\n  - `/healthz` - Basic liveness check (backward compatibility)\\n  - `/livez` - Liveness probe (can have a grace period before boot completes)\\n  - `/readyz` - Readiness probe (no grace period, must pass before serving traffic)\\n- **Dependencies checked:**\\n  - **etcd**: Separate health and readiness checks created via `CreateHealthCheck()` and `CreateReadyCheck()` in the storage factory\\n  - **Informers/Cache sync**: `NewInformerSyncHealthz` checks if shared informers have synced\\n  - **Shutdown state**: `NewShutdownHealthz` marks readiness as failed during graceful shutdown\\n  - **Post-start hooks**: Wraps hooks to fail livez until completion\\n  - **Logging**: `LogHealthz` monitors if klog is blocked\\n- Health checks can be added dynamically via `AddHealthChecks()`, `AddReadyzChecks()`, and `AddLivezChecks()`\\n- Supports grace periods for livez checks, allowing time for startup before expecting liveness\\n- Individual checks can be excluded via query parameters\\n- Supports grouped checks for category-based inclusion/exclusion\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\nGrafana implements health checking with two main endpoints: `/healthz` and `/api/health`.\\n\\n**Files:**\\n- `pkg/server/health.go` - Health notifier for managing readiness state\\n- `pkg/api/health.go` - Database health check logic\\n- `pkg/api/http_server.go` - HTTP `/api/health` - Full health endpoint that checks both liveness and database connectivity\\n- **Dependencies checked:**\\n  - **Database**: Queries the database with `SELECT 1` to verify connectivity\\n  - **Cache**: Health check result is cached for 5 seconds to avoid excessive database queries\\n  - **Version info**: Returns build version, commit, and enterprise commit (if not hidden)\\n- Returns 200 OK if database is accessible, 503 Service Unavailable if database check fails\\n- Uses `HealthNotifier` type to manage readiness state (separate from livez probe)\\n- Implements `LivezHandler()` and `ReadyzHandler()` for pod probe endpoints via `RegisterHealthEndpoints()`\\n- Simple implementation focused on database connectivity as the critical dependency\\n\\n### Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus)\\n\\nPrometheus implements health checking with two endpoints: `/-/healthy` and `/-/ready` (non-standard paths compared to Kubernetes conventions).\\n\\n**Files:**\\n- `web/web.go` - HTTP server setup and probe endpoint handlers\\n\\n**Key Features:**\\n- `/-/healthy` - Liveness probe that always returns 200 OK with message \\\"[AppName] is Healthy.\\\" (purely alive, not dependent on readiness)\\n- `/-/ready` - Readiness probe that checks if the server has completed initialization\\n- **Dependencies checked:**\\n  - **Ready status flag**: Uses atomic `ready` flag that must be explicitly set to `Ready` by the main process\\n  - **Stopping state**: Returns 503 with `X-Prometheus-Stopping: true` header when shutting down gracefully\\n  - **Initialization**: Returns 503 during startup until `SetReady(Ready)` is called\\n- Simple state-based approach: the `testReady()` wrapper function checks the `ready` status flag\\n- No built-in checks for storage, cache, or external dependencies; entirely based on manual status management\\n- The `SetReady()` function also updates a Prometheus gauge metric `readyStatus` (1 for ready, 0 for not ready)\\n- Supports HEAD requests on both endpoints for minimal overhead\\n\\n## Summary of Differences\\n\\n**Kubernetes:** Most comprehensive with pluggable health check framework, multiple endpoints with different semantics, grace period support, and extensive dependency checks (etcd, informers, logging, shutdown state).\\n\\n**Grafana:** Moderate approach with two endpoints, primary focus on database connectivity, simple caching strategy for health status.\\n\\n**Prometheus:** Minimal approach with state-based readiness, no built-in dependency checks, relies on explicit application-level state management, uses non-standard endpoint paths.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":4,"cache_creation_input_tokens":598,"cache_read_input_tokens":65239,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":598},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"06c68c4a-e76a-4ee7-9dbb-155db78ec8ee","uuid":"a2a78490-0fea-45ef-9123-3bc57b321c96"}
